pm ON t.sku_code = pm.sku_code\\n    CROSS JOIN latest_12_months l\\n    WHERE g.most_often_purchased_city_tier = 2\\n      AND t.paid_date >= l.start_date AND t.paid_date <= l.end_date\\n    GROUP BY t.sku_code, pm.class_name\\n    ORDER BY net_sales DESC\\n    LIMIT 10\\n)\\nSELECT \'Tier 1\' AS city_tier, sku_code, class_name, net_sales FROM top_products_tier1\\nUNION ALL\\nSELECT \'Tier 2\' AS city_tier, sku_code, class_name, net_sales FROM top_products_tier2\\nORDER BY city_tier, net_sales DESC;"}}', 'message_files': []}

'bc644fb5-6dc3-483a-85b8-47938e306f52', 'created_at': 1755817376, 'task_id': '767d7768-4467-4867-a046-f618eaf4259a', 'id': '54f8fab3-000e-408e-908f-1d782f677e8f', 'position': 2, 'thought': '{\n  "definition": [\n    "Net Sales: Shipped sales excluding returns & cancellations.",\n    "most_often_purchased_city_tier: Values 1, 1.5, 2, 3 indicating city tier classification."\n  ],\n  "math_formula": [],\n  "steps": [\n    "Define the latest 12-month period from 2024-07-29 to 2025-07-28 based on the available transaction data range.",\n    "Identify top-performing products by net sales (price * quantity) for Tier 1 cities (most_often_purchased_city_tier = 1).",\n    "Identify top-performing products by net sales for Tier 2 cities (most_often_purchased_city_tier = 2).",\n    "Join transaction data with guest_tagging and product_master to link sales to city tier and product category.",\n    "Aggregate net sales by sku_code and class_name, then limit to top 10 per tier.",\n    "Combine and present results separately for Tier 1 and Tier 2."\n  ],\n  "sql_query": "WITH latest_12_months AS (\\n    SELECT \'2024-07-29\' AS start_date, \'2025-07-28\' AS end_date\\n),\\ntop_products_tier1 AS (\\n    SELECT \\n        t.sku_code,\\n        pm.class_name,\\n        SUM(t.price * t.quantity) AS net_sales\\n    FROM transaction t\\n    JOIN guest_tagging g ON t.customer_code = g.customer_code\\n    JOIN product_master pm ON t.sku_code = pm.sku_code\\n    CROSS JOIN latest_12_months l\\n    WHERE g.most_often_purchased_city_tier = 1\\n      AND t.paid_date >= l.start_date AND t.paid_date <= l.end_date\\n    GROUP BY t.sku_code, pm.class_name\\n    ORDER BY net_sales DESC\\n    LIMIT 10\\n),\\ntop_products_tier2 AS (\\n    SELECT \\n        t.sku_code,\\n        pm.class_name,\\n        SUM(t.price * t.quantity) AS net_sales\\n    FROM transaction t\\n    JOIN guest_tagging g ON t.customer_code = g.customer_code\\n    JOIN product_master pm ON t.sku_code = pm.sku_code\\n    CROSS JOIN latest_12_months l\\n    WHERE g.most_often_purchased_city_tier = 2\\n      AND t.paid_date >= l.start_date AND t.paid_date <= l.end_date\\n    GROUP BY t.sku_code, pm.class_name\\n    ORDER BY net_sales DESC\\n    LIMIT 10\\n)\\nSELECT \'Tier 1\' AS city_tier, sku_code, class_name, net_sales FROM top_products_tier1\\nUNION ALL\\nSELECT \'Tier 2\' AS city_tier, sku_code, class_name, net_sales FROM top_products_tier2\\nORDER BY city_tier, net_sales DESC;",\n  "table_markdown": "|city_tier|sku_code|class_name|net_sales|\\n|---|---|---|---|\\n|Tier
